SLONG DE 'GYOD PA SKYES NAS BCOM LDAN

'DAS KYIS BKA' STZAL PA, NYES PA MED DE, SHIN TU BRTAGS LA BLANG
BAR GYIS SHIG ,DGE SLONG DE DAG GIS KYANG MI GTZANG BAS REG PA'I
PHYAG DAR KHROD KYI GOS BCANGS


@447B PA DANG, LHA PHRAN RNAMS 'PHYA NAS BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS BKA'
STZAL PA, PHYAG DAR KHROD KYI GOS NI, SHIN TU BKRUS TE LEGS PAR
BTZEMS LA BCANG BAR BYA YI, DGE SLONG DAG GIS MI

GTZANG BAS REG PA'I PHYAG DAR KHROD KYI GOS MA 'CHANG ZHIG
,'CHANG BA GANG YIN PA DE NI, NYES BYAS SU 'GYUR RO, ,DGE SLONG
DE DAG GIS BDAG PO YOD PA'I DUR KHROD NAS GOS BLANGS

PA DANG, RIGS NGAN RNAMS KYIS GANG CUNG ZAD BDAG CAG GIS LAS SU
BYA BA THAMS CAD 'DI DAG GI PHYIR BYED NA, 'DI NAS GOS MA BRKU
ZHIG ,CES DE SKAD MI SNYAN PAR SMRA BA DANG, BCOM

LDAN 'DAS KYIS BKA' STZAL PA, BDAG PO DANG BCAS PA'I DUR KHROD
NAS GOS MA LEN CIG ,BLANGS NA, NYES PA SBOM POR 'GYUR RO, ,DUR
KHROD NAS SHIN TU MI RING BA ZHIG NA LOG

PA'I LHA KHANG ZHIG YOD DE, DE NAS RAS SHIG RLUNG GIS KHYER NAS
DUR KHROD DU LHUNG BA DANG, DGE SLONG ZHIG PHYAG DAR KHROD KYI
GOS TSOL ZHING DUR KHROD DU 'ONGS PA DES RAS DE RNYED NAS

DE BLANGS TE KHYER BA DANG, LOG PA'I LHA KHANG NA GNAS PA DE DAG
GIS MTHONG NAS BTZUN PA, BDAG GI RAS 'DI LOG PA'I LHA KHANG NAS
DUR KHROD DU LHUNG BA YIN GYI, RAS 'DI

MA BRKU ZHIG ,CES SMRAS PA DANG, DE STE KHYOD KYI YIN NA, SLAR
KHYER CIG ,DGE SLONG DE 'GYOD PA SKYES NAS BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS
BKA' STZAL PA, BDAG PO GZHAN
